	focus = {
		id = CHI_first_congress_focus
		icon = GFX_goal_CHI_YUN_reconcile
		cost = 5

		x = 20
		y = 2

		ai_will_do = { base = 1000 }
		allow_branch = {
			OR = {
				CHI_is_phase_two_trigger = yes
				CHI_is_phase_three_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		available = {
			owns_state = 613
			NOT = { country_exists = LEP }
			NOT = { country_exists = ANQ }
		}
		cancel = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = CHI_focus_tree_has_changed_tt
				CHI_is_phase_four_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		select_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Select Focus CHI_first_congress_focus"
			country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.001 }
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus CHI_first_congress_focus"
			add_war_support = -0.35
			add_stability = 0.2
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_proclaim_national_revolution_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = LEP
						is_core_of = ANQ
						is_core_of = SQI
					}
					has_resistance = yes
				}
				add_compliance = 10
			}
			add_to_variable = { CHI.kr_china_provinceintegration_cost_small = -10 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI.kr_china_provinceintegration_cost_medium = -10 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI.kr_china_provinceintegration_cost_large = -10 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI.kr_china_concessionintegration_cost = -5 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI.kr_china_provinceintegration_speed = -20 }
			add_to_variable = { CHI.kr_china_concessionintegration_speed = -15 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_integration_cost_down_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_integration_time_down_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_government
				country_event = CHI.midgame.006
				set_potential_national_government = yes
				add_to_array = { china_possible_allies_array_northwest = XSM }
				add_to_array = { china_possible_allies_array_northwest = SIK }
				add_to_array = { china_possible_allies_array_northwest = MON }
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS }
	}

					add_stability = 0.10
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_form_department } }
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_form_department
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_psycho_warfare } }
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_psycho_warfare
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_anti_partisan } }
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_anti_partisan
				}
				else = { add_stability = 0.10 }
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.703 days = 15 random_days = 2 } } #Special Methods in Action
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" } }
					army_experience = 40
					if = {
						limit = {
							CHI_is_phase_four_trigger = yes
							NOT = { has_completed_focus = CHI_eyes_in_the_dark }
						}
						add_ideas = CHI_mss_idea
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training } }
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_interrogation_techniques } }
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_interrogation_techniques
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_passive_defense } }
					upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_passive_defense
				}
				else = { army_experience = 40 }
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.701 days = 15 random_days = 2 } } #Xenophobia in the MSS
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}

					max = 100
				}

			}
			if = {  #Gu Mengyu
				limit = { CHI_Gu_Mengyu_hog = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { CHI_stability_factor = ROOT.party_popularity@social_democrat }
				multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_stability_factor = 0.3 }
				clamp_temp_variable = {
					var = CHI_stability_factor
					min = 0
					max = 100
				}
				add_stability = CHI_stability_factor
			}
		}

	}
